<script type="text/javascript">
	//加载查询comboSelect
 	loadComboSelect();	

    /**
	  添加手动轨迹
	**/
   function trackList_onclick_additem() {
		var data = $("input[name='tracklist_checkbox_sid']:checked");
		if (data.length == 0) {
			alertMsg.error("请勾选信息!");
			return;
		}
		var array = "";
		for(var i = 0 ; i < data.length ; i++){
		    var dadddd = data[i].value.split(",");
			array += $.trim(dadddd[0])+",";
		}
		$.pdialog.open("/express/TrackServlet?action=initTrackItem&sids="+array, "addtrackitem", "添加手动轨迹", {width:550,height:400,mask:true});
   }
   
    /**
	  按单据添加手动轨迹
	**/
   function trackList_onclick_additembysid() {
		$.pdialog.open("/express/TrackServlet?action=initTrackItemBySid", "addtrackitembysid", "按单据添加手动轨迹", {width:550,height:450,mask:true});
   }
	/**
	 设置轨迹状态
	**/
   function trackList_onclick_setting() {
		var data = $("input[name='tracklist_checkbox_sid']:checked");
		if (data.length == 0) {
			alertMsg.error("请勾选信息!");
			return;
		}
		var array = "";
		for(var i = 0 ; i < data.length; i++){
		    var dadddd = data[i].value.split(",");
			array += $.trim(dadddd[0])+",";
		}
		$.pdialog.open("/express/TrackServlet?action=initSetStatus&sids="+array, "addtrackitem", "设置轨迹状态", {width:550,height:400,mask:true});
   }
   /**
      上传签收图片
   **/
   function trackList_onclick_setting_image() {
		var data = $("input[name='tracklist_checkbox_sid']:checked");
		if (data.length == 0) {
			alertMsg.error("请勾选信息!");
			return;
		}
		var array = "";
		for(var i = 0 ; i < data.length; i++){
		    var dadddd = data[i].value.split(",");
			array += $.trim(dadddd[0])+",";
		}
		$.pdialog.open("/express/TrackServlet?action=initUploadImage&sids="+array, "addtrackitem", "上传签收图片", {width:600,height:250,mask:true});
   }
   /**
      查看签收图片
   **/
   function trackList_onclick_check_image() {
		var data = $("input[name='tracklist_checkbox_sid']:checked");
		if (data.length == 0) {
			alertMsg.error("请勾选信息!");
			return;
		}
		var array = "";
		for(var i = 0 ; i < data.length; i++){
		    var dadddd = data[i].value.split(",");
			array += $.trim(dadddd[0])+",";
		}
		$.pdialog.open("/express/TrackServlet?action=checkUploadImage&sids="+array, "addtrackitem", "查看签收图片", {width:500,height:400,mask:true});
   }

   /**
      删除签收图片
   **/
   function trackList_onclick_delete_image() {
		var data = $("input[name='tracklist_checkbox_sid']:checked");
		if (data.length == 0) {
			alertMsg.error("请勾选信息!");
			return;
		}
		var array = "";
		for(var i = 0 ; i < data.length; i++){
		    var dadddd = data[i].value.split(",");
			array += $.trim(dadddd[0])+",";
		}
		alertMsg.confirm("你勾选了"+data.length+"条数据，确认要删除签收图片?", {
			okCall: function(){
				ajaxTodo("/express/TrackServlet?action=deleteUploadImage&sids="+array);
			}
		});
   }
   
   /**
         轨迹推送记录
   **/
   function pushTrackInfoRecord(){
   	var checkBoxs = $("input[name='tracklist_checkbox_sid']:checked"); 
   	var sids="";
   	checkBoxs.each(function(){
	  sids+=this.value+",";
   	});
   $.pdialog.open("/Order/COrder?action=vIRecordList&module=TRACK&pageflag=1&serialids="+sids,"","轨迹推送记录",{mask:true,width:1200,height:500});
	}

   function trackList_onclick_clearitem() {
		var data = $("input[name='tracklist_checkbox_sid']:checked");
		if (data.length == 0) {
			alertMsg.error("请勾选信息!");
			return;
		}
		var array = "";
		for(var i = 0 ; i < data.length ; i++){
		    var dadddd = data[i].value.split(",");
			array += $.trim(dadddd[0])+",";
		}
		alertMsg.confirm("你勾选了"+data.length+"条数据，确认要清空查件轨迹信息?", {
			okCall: function(){
				ajaxTodo("/express/TrackServlet?action=clearTrackItem&sids="+array);
			}
		});
   }

    function trackList_onclick_clearDetails() {
		var data = $("input[name='tracklist_checkbox_sid']:checked");
		if (data.length == 0) {
			alertMsg.error("请勾选信息!");
			return;
		}
		var array = "";
		for(var i = 0 ; i < data.length ; i++){
		    var dadddd = data[i].value.split(",");
			array += $.trim(dadddd[0])+",";
		}
		alertMsg.confirm("你勾选了"+data.length+"条数据，确认要清空手动轨迹信息?", {
			okCall: function(){
				ajaxTodo("/express/TrackServlet?action=clearTrackDetails&sids="+array);
			}
		});
   }

   function trackList_onclick_autoaddtrack() {
		alertMsg.confirm("自动生成轨迹信息将会删除之前轨迹，确认要自动生成轨迹信息?", {
			okCall: function(){
				ajaxTodo("/express/TrackServlet?action=startAutoTrack");
			}
		});
   }

   function trackList_onclick_list_onkeydown(e){
    if(!e) e = window.event;//火狐中是 window.event

    if((e.keyCode || e.which) == 13){
         var track_chinese=document.getElementById("track_chinese");
		 if($.trim(track_chinese.value).length != 0 ){
             getCountryXML(track_chinese,'track_country');
		 }
		 var track_clientname=document.getElementById("track_clientname");
		 if($.trim(track_clientname.value).length != 0 ){
             getClientXML(track_clientname,'track_clientid');
		 }

		 var tracklist_vendername=document.getElementById("tracklist_vendername");
		 if($.trim(tracklist_vendername.value).length != 0 ){
             getVenderXML(tracklist_vendername,'tracklist_venderid');
		 }

    }
}
   
   function deletetask(){
		$.ajax({
		    type: "POST",
		    url: "/sys/SysTask?action=delete",
		    dataType:"json",
		    success: function(json){
		   		if(json.succeed){
		     		alertMsg.correct(json.msg);
		   		}else{
		   			alertMsg.error(json.msg);
		   		}
		    }
		});
	}

//加载查询comboSelect
 loadComboSelect();
</script>
